; >>>> start of resources section <<<<
; Kull - Added resource conversion section below as a reference (also see descr_sm_resources.txt)
;
; gold = EBII Gold
; silver = EBII Silver
; fish = EBII Gems
; tin = EBII Tin
; coal = EBII Copper
; iron = EBII Iron
; sulfur = EBII Lead
; amber = EBII Amber
; tobacco = EBII Incense
; silk = EBII Slaves
; dyes = EBII Special Dyes
; marble = EBII Marble / Granite
; elephants = EBII Pitch
; timber = EBII Specialized Timber
; camels = EBII Exotic Animals
; dogs = EBII Warhorses
; ivory = EBII Elephants/Ivory
; chocolate = EBII Livestock
; spices = EBII Spices
; cotton = EBII Olives
; wine = EBII Wine
; sugar = EBII Honey
; wool = EBII Salt
; grain = EBII Major Grain Production
; furs = EBII Local Trade
; slaves = EBII PSF
;
; Note that some areas have got commented resources not because of not having them, but because
; of the fact that when all the provinces in a region have the same type of resource -olives in greece,
; for instance-, they don´t trade it between each other. Thus, some resources have been limited inside
; the area, to encourage trade.
; -Praetor-
